The term [3mmarket cap [0mrefers to the total market capitalization of a publicly traded company (price of the stock times numbers of 
shares outstanding). A market-cap index is a stock index where stocks are ranked according to their market-cap size. 
Dividend-weight index refers to an index that is ranked according to the dividend each company pays.
